	ftruncate(fd, sizeof(int));
	void* addr = mmap(NULL, sizeof(int), PROT_READ|PROT_WRITE,
		MAP_SHARED, fd, 0);
	if (addr == MAP_FAILED)
		perror("ERREUR MAP_FAILED");
	printf("addr: %p\n", addr);
	sem_init(&sem1, 0, 1);
	sem_init(&sem2, 0, 0);
	sem_init(&sem3, 0, 0);
	pthread_t tA, tB;
	pthread_create(&tA, NULL, A, addr);
	pthread_create(&tB, NULL, B, addr);
	for (i = 1; i <= 150; i++)
		sem_wait(&sem1);
		memcpy(addr, &i, sizeof i); 
		sem_post(&sem2);
	ok = 0;
	pthread_join(tA, NULL);
	pthread_join(tB, NULL);
	return 0;

    pthread_create(&thB, NULL, (void *)threadB, NULL);
    pthread_join(thB, NULL);
    pthread_join(thA, NULL);
    return 0;

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <pthread.h>
#include <semaphore.h>
#define NO_PLACES 5
#define NO_CARS 7
#define NO_ENTRIES 2
#define NO_EXITS 2
sem_t libre, entree, sortie;
pthread_mutex_t mutex = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER;
void enterParking(int carId) {
  int placeLibre, porte;
  sem_wait(&libre);
  pthread_mutex_lock(&mutex); 
  sem_getvalue(&libre, &placeLibre);
  sem_getvalue(&entree, &porte);
  pthread_mutex_unlock(&mutex); 
  printf("[%d] entre porte %d, il reste %d places libre\n", carId, porte, placeLibre);
void leaveParking(int carId){
  int porte;
  sem_post(&libre);
  pthread_mutex_lock(&mutex); 
  sem_getvalue(&sortie, &porte);
  pthread_mutex_unlock(&mutex); 
  printf("[%d] sort à la porte %d\n", carId, porte);
void * carLife(void * carId){
  int * id = (int *) carId;
  int sec, busy;
  srandom(RAND_MAX);
  sem_wait(&entree);
  enterParking(*id);
  sem_post(&entree);
  sec = random()%10+1;
  printf("[%d] reste %ds\n",*id,sec);
  sleep(sec);
  sem_wait(&sortie);
  leaveParking(*id);
  sem_post(&sortie);
  pthread_exit(NULL);
int main(int argc, char const *argv[]) {
  pthread_t cars[NO_CARS];
  int id[NO_CARS] = {0,1,2,3,4,5,6};
  int i;
  sem_init(&libre,0,NO_PLACES);
  sem_init(&entree,0,NO_ENTRIES);
  sem_init(&sortie,0,NO_EXITS);
  for (i = 0; i < NO_CARS; i++) {
    pthread_create(&cars[i], NULL, carLife, &id[i]);
  for (i = 0; i < NO_CARS; i++) {
    pthread_join(cars[i], NULL);
  return 0;

/Users/Laure/Downloads/TPS/poize/TP1/q5.c(7)
/Users/Laure/Downloads/TPS/poize/TP2/q1_b.c(79)
int creeSegment(int taille, char *nom, int cle)
	int shmid ; 
	key_t clef ; 
	clef = ftok(nom,(key_t) cle) ;
	shmid = shmget( clef,taille,IPC_CREAT|IPC_EXCL|SHM_R|SHM_W ) ;
	if ( shmid== -1 ) 
		perror("La creation du segment de memoire partage a echouee") ;
		exit(1) ; 
	printf("l'identificateur du segment est %d \n",shmid) ;
	printf("ce segment est associe a la clef %d \n",clef) ;
	return shmid ;

	printf("A%d ",var_glob);
	val = var_glob;
sem_post(&mutexB);
void * impair(void *arg){
int val = -1;
while(1)
sem_wait(&mutexB);
if(var_glob%2&&val!=var_glob)
	printf("B%d ",var_glob);
	val = var_glob;

	sem_init(&mutexB,0,1);

	pthread_create(&threadB,NULL,impair,NULL);
	while(var_glob<1000)

		var_glob++;

	pthread_cancel(threadB);
return 0;

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <pthread.h>
#include <semaphore.h>
#define NO_PLACES 5
#define NO_CARS 7
#define NO_ENTRIES 2
#define NO_EXITS 2
sem_t libre, entree, sortie;
pthread_mutex_t mutex = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER;
void enterParking(int carId){
  int placeLibre, porte;
  sem_wait(&libre);
  pthread_mutex_lock(&mutex); 
  sem_getvalue(&libre, &placeLibre);
  sem_getvalue(&entree, &porte);
  pthread_mutex_unlock(&mutex); 
  printf("[%d] entre porte %d, il reste %d places libre\n", carId, porte, placeLibre);
void leaveParking(int carId){
  int porte;
  sem_post(&libre);
  pthread_mutex_lock(&mutex); 
  sem_getvalue(&sortie, &porte);
  pthread_mutex_unlock(&mutex); 
  printf("[%d] sort à la porte %d\n", carId, porte);
void * carLife(void * carId){
  int * id = (int *) carId;
  int sec, busy;
  srandom(RAND_MAX);
  sem_wait(&entree);
  enterParking(*id);
  sem_post(&entree);
  sec = random()%10+1;
  printf("[%d] reste %ds\n",*id,sec);
  sleep(sec);
  sem_wait(&sortie);
  leaveParking(*id);
  sem_post(&sortie);
  pthread_exit(NULL);
int main(int argc, char const *argv[]) {
  pthread_t cars[NO_CARS];
  int id[NO_CARS] = {0,1,2,3,4,5,6};
  int i;
  sem_init(&libre,0,NO_PLACES);
  sem_init(&entree,0,NO_ENTRIES);
  sem_init(&sortie,0,NO_EXITS);
  for (i = 0; i < NO_CARS; i++) {
    pthread_create(&cars[i], NULL, carLife, &id[i]);
  for (i = 0; i < NO_CARS; i++) {
    pthread_join(cars[i], NULL);
  return 0;

int creeSegment(int taille, char* nom, int key)
	 int shmid ; 
	 key_t cle ; 
  	cle = ftok(nom,(key_t) key) ;
  shmid = shmget( cle,taille,IPC_CREAT|IPC_EXCL|SHM_R|SHM_W ) ;
  if ( shmid== -1 ) {
    	perror("La creation du segment de memoire partage a echouee") ;
    	exit(1) ; 
	printf("l'identificateur du segment est %d \n",shmid) ;
  	printf("ce segment est associe a la clef %d \n",cle) ;
  	return shmid ;

void fume(char* idFumeur, char* idFournisseur){
     printf("++++++le fumeur %s fume et libere le fournisseur %s\n", idFumeur, idFournisseur);
     if(idFournisseur == "X"){
          sem_post(&semaphore_fournisseurX);
          if(idFumeur == "A"){
               sem_post(&semaphore_allumettes);
          else if(idFumeur == "B"){
               sem_post(&semaphore_tabac);
          else if(idFumeur == "C"){
               sem_post(&semaphore_tabac);
               sem_post(&semaphore_allumettes);
     else if(idFournisseur == "Y"){
          sem_post(&semaphore_fournisseurY);

char *creeSegment(int memSize, char *memFileName, int id) {
    char *memory = NULL;
    id = shm_open(memFileName, O_RDWR|O_CREAT, 0600);
    if (id == -1) {
        printf("Erreur shm_open()\n");
        exit(1);
    if (ftruncate(id, memSize) == -1) {
        printf("Erreur ftruncate()\n");
        exit(1);
    memory = (char*)mmap(NULL, memSize, PROT_READ|PROT_WRITE, MAP_SHARED, id, 0);
	if (memory == MAP_FAILED) {
        printf("Erreur mmap()\n");
        exit(1);
	printf("Mémoire : %s\n", memory);
	printf("ID : %d\n", id);
	return memory;

#include <fcntl.h>           
char *creeSegment(int memSize, char *memFileName, int id) {
    char *memory = NULL;
    id = shm_open(memFileName, O_RDWR|O_CREAT, 0600);
    if (id == -1) {
        printf("Erreur shm_open()\n");
        exit(1);
    if (ftruncate(id, memSize) == -1) {
        printf("Erreur ftruncate()\n");
        exit(1);
    memory = (char*)mmap(NULL, memSize, PROT_READ|PROT_WRITE, MAP_SHARED, id, 0);
	if (memory == MAP_FAILED) {
        printf("Erreur mmap()\n");
        exit(1);
	printf("Mémoire : %s\n", memory);
	printf("ID : %d\n", id);
	return memory;
void fermerSegment(int memSize, char *memFileName, int id, char *partage) {
    if (munmap(partage, memSize) == -1) {
        printf("Erreur munmap()\n");
        exit(1);
    close(id);
    if(shm_unlink(memFileName) == -1) {
        printf("Erreur shm_unlink()\n");

int creeSegment(int size, char *name, int cle){
  int shmid ; 
  key_t clef ; 
  clef = ftok(name,(key_t) cle) ;
  shmid = shmget( clef, size, IPC_CREAT|IPC_EXCL|SHM_R|SHM_W ) ;
  if ( shmid== -1 )
    perror("La creation du segment de memoire partage a echouee") ;
    exit(1) ; 
  printf("l'identificateur du segment est %d \n",shmid) ;
  printf("ce segment est associe a la clef %d \n",clef) ;
  return shmid ;

#include <sys/ipc.h>
#include <sys/shm.h>
int creeSegment(int size, char *name, int cle){
  int shmid ; 
  key_t clef ; 
  clef = ftok(name,(key_t) cle) ;
  shmid = shmget( clef, size, IPC_CREAT|IPC_EXCL|SHM_R|SHM_W ) ;
  if ( shmid== -1 )
    perror("La creation du segment de memoire partage a echouee") ;
    exit(1) ; 
  printf("l'identificateur du segment est %d \n",shmid) ;
  printf("ce segment est associe a la clef %d \n",clef) ;
  return shmid ;
void detruitSegment(int shmid)
  if (shmctl(shmid,IPC_RMID,NULL) == -1)
    perror("Erreur lors de la destruction") ;
    exit(1) ;

int creeSegment(int size, char *name, int cle){
  int shmid ; 
  key_t clef ; 
  clef = ftok(name,(key_t) cle) ;
  shmid = shmget( clef, size, IPC_CREAT|IPC_EXCL|SHM_R|SHM_W ) ;
  if ( shmid== -1 )
    perror("La creation du segment de memoire partage a echouee") ;
    exit(1) ; 
  printf("l'identificateur du segment est %d \n",shmid) ;
  printf("ce segment est associe a la clef %d \n",clef) ;
  return shmid ;
void detruitSegment(int shmid)
  if (shmctl(shmid,IPC_RMID,NULL) == -1)
    perror("Erreur lors de la destruction") ;
    exit(1) ;

	sem_post(&p1_sem);
int main (void)
	int fd = shm_open("/regint", O_CREAT | O_RDWR, S_IRUSR
		| S_IWUSR);
	ftruncate(fd, sizeof(int)); 
	void* addr = mmap(NULL, sizeof(int), PROT_READ|PROT_WRITE,
		MAP_SHARED, fd, 0);
	if (addr == MAP_FAILED)
		perror("ERREUR MAP_FAILED");
	printf("addr: %p\n", addr);
	sem_init(&p1_sem, 0, 1);
	sem_init(&p2_sem, 0, 0);
	sem_init(&p3_sem, 0, 0);
	pthread_t tA, tB;
	pthread_create(&tA, NULL, A, addr);
	pthread_create(&tB, NULL, B, addr);
	for (int i = 1; i <= 1000; i++)
		sem_wait(&p1_sem);
		memcpy(addr, &i, sizeof i); 
		sem_post(&p2_sem);
	ok = 0;
	pthread_join(tA, NULL);
	pthread_join(tB, NULL);
	return 0;

#include <stdio.h>

#define NO_PLACES 5 
#define NO_CARS 10 
#define NO_ENTRIES 3 
#define NO_EXITS 2 
sem_t places_libre_sem;
sem_t entrees_libre_sem;
sem_t sorties_libre_sem;
pthread_mutex_t assign_deb_mut = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER;
pthread_mutex_t assign_fin_mut = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER;
void enterParking(int carId)
	printf("Arrivee de n°%d.\n", carId);
	sem_wait(&entrees_libre_sem);
	printf("n°%d Attend a l'entree.\n", carId);
	sem_wait(&places_libre_sem);
	printf("n°%d entre (1sec).\n", carId);
	sleep(1);
	sem_post(&entrees_libre_sem);
void leaveParking(int carId)
	printf("n°%d Attends pour sortir.\n", carId);
	sem_wait(&sorties_libre_sem);
	printf("n°%d sort (1sec).\n", carId);
	sleep(1);
	sem_post(&sorties_libre_sem);
	sem_post(&places_libre_sem);
	printf("n°%d est sortie.\n", carId);
void *carLife(void* carId)
	pthread_mutex_lock(&assign_deb_mut);
	int id = (*(int*)carId);
	pthread_mutex_unlock(&assign_fin_mut);
	enterParking(id);
	sleep(random()%5);
	leaveParking(id);

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <sys/types.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <pthread.h>
void *A(void* message)
	for (int i = 2; i <= 1000; i+=2)
		printf("A %d\n", i);
void *B(void* message)
	for (int i = 1; i <= 999; i+=2)
		printf("B %d\n", i);
int main (void)
	pthread_t tA, tB;
	pthread_create(&tA, NULL, A, NULL);
	pthread_create(&tB, NULL, B, NULL);
	pthread_join(tA, NULL);
	pthread_join(tB, NULL);
	return 0;

	char cars[strlen(chaine)];

	fils2 = fork();

		if(chaine[i] == '0' || chaine[i] == '1' || chaine[i] == '2'

			|| chaine[i] == '6' || chaine[i] == '7' || chaine[i] == '8' || chaine[i] == '9'){

				char mess[100];
				mess[0] = chaine[i];
				write(fd[W], mess, 101);
				printf("pere1:%c\n", mess[0]);
			if(fils1 == 0){
				while(1){
					read(fd[R], recu_fils, 101);
					somme += recu_fils[0]-'0';
					printf("fils1:%c, %i, %i\n", recu_fils[0], somme, recu_fils[0]-'0');
				exit(0);
		else{
			if(fils1 != 0 && fils2 != 0){
				char mess[100];
				mess[0] = chaine[i];
				write(fd2[W], mess, 101);
				printf("pere2:%c\n", mess[0]);
			if(fils2 == 0){
				while(1){
					read(fd2[R], recu_fils, 101);
					printf("fils2:%c\n", recu_fils[0]);
				exit(0);
	printf("\n");
	return 0;

		return EXIT_FAILURE;

void *TriBulle(void * tab)
  int i,j,tmp ;
  for (i=TAILLE-1 ; i >=0 ; --i)
    for ( j=1 ; j<=i ; j++) 
      if (((int*) tab)[j-1]>((int *) tab)[j])
        tmp       = ((int *)tab)[j-1] ;
        ((int *)tab)[j-1] = ((int *)tab)[j] ;
        ((int *)tab)[j]   = tmp ;

char * creeSegment(int mem_len, char *filename, int fd){

	char *partage = NULL;

char * creeSegment(int mem_len, char *filename, int fd){
	int res;
	char *partage = NULL;
	fd = shm_open(filename, O_RDWR|O_CREAT, 0600);
	if (fd==-1) { perror("shm_open"); exit(1); }
	res = ftruncate(fd, mem_len);
	if (res == -1) { perror("ftruncate"); exit(1); }
	partage = (char*)mmap(NULL, mem_len, PROT_READ|PROT_WRITE, MAP_SHARED, fd, 0);
	if (partage == MAP_FAILED) { perror("mmap"); exit(1); }
	printf("%s\n", partage);
	printf("%d\n", fd);
	return partage;
void fermerSegment(int mem_len, char *filename, int fd, char *partage){
	int res;
	res = munmap(partage, mem_len);
	if (res == -1) { perror("munmap"); exit(1); }
	close(fd);
	res = shm_unlink(filename); 
	if (res==-1) { perror("shm_unlink"); exit(1); }
